She's just a perfect kickass heroine with the perfect amount of sarcasm, fierceness, bravery and compassion. It's also easier to connect to her, as I struggled (still do) with Mercy. Overall, this series is awesome with an interesting conc</span>
  <span id="freeText9736802942535636388" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Fifth re-read: 16.07.19</u>
</b><br>I just had to re-read this book (maybe series, we'll see) again after reading <b>
  <i>Mercy Thompson</i>
</b>. This series beats MT by a whole lot. Mercy and Kate are so alike, yet so different, and it's the difference I like the most about Kate. She's just a perfect kickass heroine with the perfect amount of sarcasm, fierceness, bravery and compassion. It's also easier to connect to her, as I struggled (still do) with Mercy. Overall, this series is awesome with an interesting concept and great characters. Curran is just so damn hot.<br><b>New Rate</b>: 3.5 stars<br> <br><b><u>CHARACTERS</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Kate Daniels</b> (24), the main protagonist of the series. Kate is the POV that main story told from. <br>→ <b>Curran ‘The Beast Lord’ ‘Lord of the Free beasts’ Lennart</b> (early 30s?), the leader of The Pack located in Atlanta , which is the second largest of the shape-shifter packs in North America. He is unique among other shape-shifter Alphas being the leader of multiple types of shape-shifters. <br>→ <b>Greg Feldman</b>, former Knight-Diviner. Guardian of Kate. <br>→ <b>Beatrice ‘Aunt B’</b>, Alpha of Clan Bouda. Mother of <b>Raphael Medrano</b>.<br>→ <b>Derek Gaunt</b>, a teenaged werewolf who is one of Kate's closest friends and a protégé of both Jim and Curran.<br>→ <b>Jim Shrapshire</b>, the Chief of Security for The Pack, the Alpha Male of Clan Cat, a part-time Merc, and a close friend of Curran and the closest thing to a partner Kate had; once in a while they shared merc jobs from the Guild. <br>→ <b>Saiman</b>, <br>→ <b>Dr. George Doolittle</b>, werebadger. Pack Medmage.<br>→ <b>Mahon Delany</b>, werebear. Alpha of Clan Heavy. The Kodiak of Atlanta, the Pack executioner. Husband of <b>Martha</b>, father of <b>George</b>. Raised Curran as his own son.<br>→ <b>Ghastek Stefanoff</b>, Atlanta’s premier Master of the Dead. (People)<br>→ <b>Rowena</b>, Master of the Dead. (People)<br>→ <b>Ted Moynohan</b>, Knight Protector. One of the original founders of The Order. Bigoted against non-humans. <br>→ <b>Maxine</b>, receptionist with the Order of Merciful Aid for over 25 years. Exceptionally strong telepath. Middle-aged and intimidating.<br>→ <b>Nataraja</b>, the local lord/leader of the People in Atlanta. Uncanny sensitivity to magic. The People are Necromancers who pilot and control Vampires.<br>→ <b>Roland</b>, the legendary leader of the People. It’s rumored that he’s been alive since magic last left the world, which was about four thousand years ago. He’s supposed to have incredible power, almost godlike. Some say he’s Merlin, some say he’s Gilgamesh. He has some sort of agenda and uses the People to achieve it, although the majority of them have never seen him. There’s no proof of his existence and lay people like Derek and Kate aren’t suppose to know about him.<br>→ <b>Jennifer Hinton</b>, the female alpha-wolf, mated to wolf-alpha <b>Daniel</b>.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>

<div id="review_550570811" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550570811" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550570811?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/7940930-magic-bites">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2015-read">2015-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2014-read">2014-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550570811" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12824042275137560051">2 March 2020: <a href='https://amzn.to/38hOIOT' rel='nofollow noopener'>$0.99 on Kindle</a><br/><br/>May 2016 Re-read: I love this book. I love this world. I love Kate. It's still my favorite series. It's fantastic, it's a great start, and if you haven't read it yet, DO IT. And then remember that the books just get better from here, exponentially better. <br/><br/>June 2015 Re-read: This is the series I go to when I need to reboot myself. I love it. Each time I read it, I love it a little bit more.<br/><br/>July re-read: Is it possible for a series to get better and better with each re</span>
  <span id="freeText12824042275137560051" style="display:none">2 March 2020: <a href="https://amzn.to/38hOIOT" rel="nofollow noopener">$0.99 on Kindle</a><br /><br />May 2016 Re-read: I love this book. I love this world. I love Kate. It's still my favorite series. It's fantastic, it's a great start, and if you haven't read it yet, DO IT. And then remember that the books just get better from here, exponentially better. <br /><br />June 2015 Re-read: This is the series I go to when I need to reboot myself. I love it. Each time I read it, I love it a little bit more.<br /><br />July re-read: Is it possible for a series to get better and better with each re-read? Apparently the answer is YES!!!<br /><br />20 July 2014: <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B000SEH16E/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B000SEH16E&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=touthenig-20&amp;linkId=FABP2VJUPJ65ATIC" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99 on Kindle</a><br /><br />This is my favorite series ever - the first book, some people have trouble with (I loved it from the start), but it's SO worth it!!! The entire series is on sale!!!<br /><br /><br />Review:<br />Kate Daniels is a mercenary for the Guild. She’s having a bit of trouble making ends meet when she gets a visit suggesting that she get in contact with her guardian. But when she tries she gets stonewalled. And then she finds out he’s dead, killed by an apparently unknown magical being. <br /><br />Now Kate’s on the job, searching for the answers, which brings her into contact with some of the most powerful beings in Atlanta. She’ll travel from the heart of the vampire’s power, the People’s Casino, to the shapeshifter’s Keep, ruled by the Beast Lord and everywhere in between.<br /><br />I read this book quite a while ago, finally, at the insistence of one of my best friends – who had been recommending the series to me for over a year! What on earth took me so long? I’m doing this review now because I just got done listening to the audiobook and wanted to comment on both.<br /><br />First, I absolutely love Kate. Not only does she kick ass and have a smart mouth, but because when she does talk, she can back it up – unless she’s trying to aggravate Curran of course. She’s not perfect, she makes mistakes, she has flaws! Sometimes she even makes rash decisions. And this is probably one of my favorite things about her – when she does any of the above, it doesn’t always turn out the way she wants and sometimes she has to accept the consequences of her actions. I’ll say it again, because I think it’s something that’s missing in a lot of urban fantasy I read – Kate’s (and truly all the characters) actions have consequences and they don’t just go away, they have to be dealt with. And it’s not always easy. Another thing to love about Kate is that she has a personal code of conduct, and she sticks to it. Honestly, there’s not one thing I didn’t love about Kate. Impressive, considering how difficult it is to make me truly like a heroine.<br /><br />Now, I’ve spent all this time talking about Kate and haven’t mentioned a single other character. And there are so many wonderful characters to mention. Curran, I can’t even describe how much I love Curran, the Beast Lord of Atlanta. Strong, sexy, dominating, fierce. He’s arrogant and eminently sure of himself – with good cause. I was immediately enamored of him. <br /><br />Honestly, I can’t do justice to all the well-developed characters in this book, so I’ll just say that all of them are fully three-dimensional and intriguing.<br /><br />Magic Bites moves at a very quick pace, with lots of action set in a fabulously complex, detailed world. The world is a character all itself. I love the idea of the magic and tech asserting themselves at ever-changing intervals and the effects that has on our protagonist. The world building was flawlessly integrated into the story, and I never got hopelessly lost in it, though I was completely immersed. <br /><br />I highly recommend this series if you haven’t started it already. Magic Bites a rocket-fast story, set in a vivid, ever-changing world with characters that fairly jump off the page and make you beg for more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12824042275137560051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1628996255" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1628996255" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1628996255?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1628996255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2821025616970702189"><b>1st read - May 2011</b><br/><b>2nd read - June 2013</b><br/><b>3rd read - April 2015</b><br/><b>4th read - May 2016</b><br/><b>5th read - March 2017</b><br/><b>6th read - November 2017</b><br/><b>7th read - July 2018</b><br/><b>8th read - May 2019</b><br/><b>9th read - October 2020</b><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>In Magic Bites we are introduced to an interesting new world where magic and technology can't coexist. When the magic is high electronics everywhere start to fail and with the magic levels constantly fluctuating it is impossible to rely on technology to keep you safe. We are also treated to an unus</span>
  <span id="freeText2821025616970702189" style="display:none"><b>1st read - May 2011</b><br /><b>2nd read - June 2013</b><br /><b>3rd read - April 2015</b><br /><b>4th read - May 2016</b><br /><b>5th read - March 2017</b><br /><b>6th read - November 2017</b><br /><b>7th read - July 2018</b><br /><b>8th read - May 2019</b><br /><b>9th read - October 2020</b><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />In Magic Bites we are introduced to an interesting new world where magic and technology can't coexist. When the magic is high electronics everywhere start to fail and with the magic levels constantly fluctuating it is impossible to rely on technology to keep you safe. We are also treated to an unusual form of vampires - these aren't your sexy vamps that appear frequently in urban fantasy but are instead evil beings who are constantly in a state of blood lust and are only able to function under the control of a necromancer. They certainly make lethal pets and I have to admit the necromancers are almost as scary!<br /><br />Main character Kate Daniels is a loner, she has a few trusted colleagues but doesn't make friends easily and prefers to do things her own way. As a magic user she could choose to work for the Order of Knights, an organisation that offers aid to people with magical problems, but not one to stick to the rules she is happier as a mercenary drifting from job to job. When her guardian is murdered she is determined to track down his killer but with clues pointing to both the necromancers and the pack (shape shifters of all kinds) she doesn't know where to start. It looks like she may have to turn to the Order of Knights for assistance if she wants to figure things out. With disappearances amongst both the pack and the necromancers each are blaming the other and look to be on the verge of war. Kate must discover who is to blame before humans get caught in the crossfire.<br /><br />Like any first book in a series there is a lot of time spent setting the scene and introducing us to the world which meant the first part of the book is a little on the slow side but the action really picks up towards the end and made for a thoroughly enjoyable read. I liked Kate but I was particularly intrigued by Curran, the leader of the pack. I've heard a lot of good things about Curran and although we don't know a lot about him at the moment I have high hopes for future books. There is definitely chemistry between him &amp; Kate but I liked the fact that this wasn't over done in the first instalment and gives us something to look forward to as the series progresses. Magic Bites is a promising start to a series and I'm looking forward to reading more, we have a lot more to discover about Kate and the world she lives in and I'm sure it will be an interesting journey!<br /><br />_______________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />Originally read in May 2010 but re-read in June 2013 before carrying on with the rest of the series.<br /><br />I'm not writing another review but I loved it just as much, if not more, the 2nd time around. I can't believe I never got around to reading the rest of the series before but I'm looking forward to doing it now :o)<br /><br />_______________________<br /><br /><b>3rd Read</b><br /><br />I'm taking part in a mass reread of this series with the lovely peeps from the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA) Group</a><br /><br />Anyone is welcome to join us &amp; here is the reading schedule if you want to take part:<br />→ Magic Bites - April 27<br />→ Magic Burns - May 11<br />→ Magic Strikes - May 25<br />→ Magic Bleeds - Jun 8<br />→ Magic Slays - Jun 22<br />→ Magic Rises - July 6<br />→ Magic Breaks - July 20<br />→ Magic Shifts - Aug 4 <br /><br />Third time reading Magic Bites and I loved it just as much (probably more) this time around. This series is definitely one of my favourites and I can't wait to reread the rest of the books!<br /><br />_______________________<br /><br /><b>4th Read</b><br /><br />So begins the great Kate Daniels series reread of 2016 with my fellow <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts</a>!<br /><br />I love this series more with every reread! I will NEVER get enough of this world or these characters. Kate kicks arse, Curran I just adore and that's without mentioning Derek, Julie, Andrea, Doolittle and so many others! The hardest thing about this group reread is going to be sticking to the one book every 2 weeks schedule, I could quite happily binge read the entire series + all the extra shorts and novellas in a week LOL.<br /><br />_______________________<br /><br /><b>5th Read</b><br /><br />I'm still fairly new to audiobooks, I tend to get distracted when listening to them so I easily lose my place and often realise I've completely blanked on the last 10 minutes of the recording. If there is one series I'm completely addicted to it's the Kate Daniels series though so when <b>Ilona Andrews</b> was offering review copies of <b>Magic Bites</b> on Audible I jumped at the chance of giving it a try. I'm happy to say that even though I've read this book multiple times in other formats I was still just as hooked on the story this time around and it was able to hold my attention more than any other audiobook I've tried listening to.<br /><br />I thought <b>Renée Raudman</b> did a great job of bringing the characters to life. I always find it a bit weird when you have a woman voicing a male character (or equally a man voicing a female character) but it wasn't jarring enough to pull me out of the story and I quickly got used to the accents she used. I enjoyed it enough that I'm very tempted to sign up for audible and download the rest of the series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2821025616970702189" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5opTTOtD6gE170vFrpUh5h/B1QiBW/ubXkUgI1O8hxOv01rR1D8igpdKuE9moTQDwz/JUd7/kYeSsqTOqbJ9kQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7aQm9IHsEduk+nBmiQkx47oo6U4jXvnxtgchbztdBy2k/S9pvpDZWAZfg+xBPSQGZtb1F3z6k+168KWCwVP9rw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16792070016665743836">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade</span>
  <span id="freeText16792070016665743836" style="display:none">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade. (Gordon is still sore about that.)<br /><br />Gordon and Ilona currently reside in Oregon with their two children, three dogs and a cat. They have co-authored two series, the bestselling urban fantasy of Kate Daniels and romantic urban fantasy of The Edge.<br /></span>
